# Session — 2026-05-02

## Commits

### 15:53 — Narad [`962c59e`]
**feat: Phase 0a — Narad routing accuracy spike**

Sets up the test harness to validate whether Gemma 4 E4B can route user
tasks to the correct avatar(s) with reliable structured output.

Components:
- narad_schema.py: Pydantic routing schema (NaradRouting) with token-level
  grammar enforcement via outlines. Invalid JSON is impossible to emit.
- narad_claude.py: Claude Sonnet baseline evaluator using tool-use API for
  guaranteed structured output. Target: ≥95% weighted accuracy.
- narad_local.py: mlx-lm + outlines evaluator for local Gemma 4B on Apple
  Silicon. Target: ≥80% weighted accuracy (escalate if <70%).
- test_prompts.json: 50 ground-truth labelled prompts across all 7 avatars,
  multi-avatar scenarios, and edge cases.
- run_evaluation.py: CLI harness with per-category breakdown, go/no-go
  verdict, and Claude-vs-local comparison report.

Definition of done: zero parse failures (outlines enforces schema), local
accuracy ≥80% or escalate to 27B MoE.

Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>

### 16:12 — Narad [`021fef5`]
**feat: add GPT-4o baseline evaluator**

narad_openai.py uses client.beta.chat.completions.parse() with the
NaradRouting Pydantic model — same structured output guarantee as the
Claude tool-use path but uses OPENAI_API_KEY instead.

run_evaluation.py now accepts --model gpt, --model claude, or --model local.
compare_results() auto-detects whichever baseline file exists (gpt or claude).

Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>

### 16:38 — Narad [`8dfe06f`]
**fix: outlines 1.x mlxlm API + tighten Rama/Krishna/Buddha boundaries**

narad_local.py: from_mlxlm(model, tokenizer) replaces om.mlxlm(model_id)
which was renamed in outlines 1.x.

narad_schema.py: GPT-4o baseline revealed Rama/Krishna boundary leak on
every SOP task and Buddha/Krishna confusion on evaluation tasks. Tightened
system prompt descriptions to clarify:
- Rama owns all structured-sequence outputs (no Krishna just for readability)
- Krishna is specifically for persuasive/stakeholder prose
- Buddha is specifically for analytical judgement, not general review
- Parashurama handles full implementation without forced Rama/Buddha additions

Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>

Files changed:
```
M	phase-0a/narad_local.py
M	phase-0a/narad_schema.py
```

### 17:21 — Narad [`0a9bfdd`]
**fix: parse string output from outlines SteerableGenerator into NaradRouting**

outlines 1.x SteerableGenerator returns a JSON string, not a Pydantic
instance. Added isinstance branching: str->model_validate_json,
dict->model_validate, else pass through.

Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>

